Enhance component

MudAutocomplete

   186	        public async Task SetTextAsync(string? text)
   187	        {
   188	            if (!HasMask)
   189	            {
   190	                await InputReference.SetText(text);
   191	                return;
   192	            }
   193	
   194	            await _maskReference.Clear();
   195	            await _maskReference.OnPasteAsync(text);
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        /// <summary>
   199	        /// Returns the current caret position.
   200	        /// </summary>
   201	        /// <remarks>
   202	        /// Returns the text length if called and this field hasn't been focused yet.
   203	        /// Returns <c>-1</c> if called before this component has been rendered.
   204	        /// </remarks>
   205	        public async Task<int> GetCurrentCaretPositionAsync()
   206	        {
   207	            if (IsJSRuntimeAvailable && InputReference != null)
   208	            {
   209	                return await JsRuntime.InvokeAsync<int>("mudInput.getCaretPosition", InputReference.ElementReference);
   210	            }
   211	
   212	            return -1;
   213	        }
   214	
   215	        /// <summary>
   216	        /// Inserts the given text at the given caret position.
   217	        /// </summary>
   218	        /// <param name="text">The text to insert.</param>
   219	        /// <param name="position">The position to insert the text at. Set to <c>0</c> to insert the text before and to <c>int.MaxValue</c> after the existing text.</param>
   220	        /// <remarks>
   221	        /// If <c>position</c> is greater than the current text length, the text will be inserted at the end.<br/>
   222	        /// If <c>position</c> is less than <c>0</c>, the text will be inserted at the beginning.<br/>
   223	        /// Note that this function doesn't support <see cref="MudMask"/>.
   224	        /// </remarks>
   225	        public async Task InsertTextAsync(string text, int position = int.MaxValue)
   226	        {
   227	            if (HasMask)
   228	            {
   229	                throw new InvalidOperationException("Cannot insert text into masked input.");
   230	            }
   231	
   232	            if (IsJSRuntimeAvailable && InputReference != null)
   233	            {
   234	                await JsRuntime.InvokeVoidAsyncWithErrorHandling("mudInput.insertAtPosition", InputReference.ElementReference, text, position);
   235	            }
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        /// <summary>
   239	        /// Inserts the given text at the current caret position.
   240	        /// </summary>
   241	        /// <param name="text">The text to insert.</param>
   242	        public async Task InsertTextAtCurrentCaretPositionAsync(string text)
   243	        {
   244	            if (!HasMask && IsJSRuntimeAvailable && InputReference != null)
   245	            {
   246	                await JsRuntime.InvokeVoidAsyncWithErrorHandling("mudInput.insertAtCurrentCaretPosition", InputReference.ElementReference, text);
   247	                return;
   248	            }
   249	
   250	            if (HasMask)
   251	            {
   252	                await _maskReference.OnPasteAsync(text);
   253	            }
   254	        }
   255	
   256	        /// <inheritdoc />
   257	        protected override Task SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(T? value, bool updateText = true, bool force = false)
   258	        {
   259	            if (HasMask)
   260	            {
   261	                var textValue = ConvertSet(value);
   262	                _mask.SetText(textValue);
   263	                textValue = Mask.GetCleanText();
   264	                value = ConvertGet(textValue);
   265	            }
   266	
   267	            return base.SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(value, updateText, force);
   268	        }
   269	
   270	        /// <inheritdoc />
   271	        protected override Task SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(string? text, bool updateValue = true)
   272	        {
   273	            if (HasMask)
   274	            {
   275	                _mask.SetText(text);
   276	                text = _mask.Text;
   277	            }
   278	
   279	            return base.SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(text, updateValue);
   280	        }

   283	        protected internal override InputType GetInputType() => InputType;
   284	
   285	        private bool ShowClearButton()
   286	        {
   287	            if (SubscribeToParentForm)
   288	                return Clearable && !GetReadOnlyState() && !GetDisabledState();
   289	            return Clearable && !GetDisabledState();
   290	        }
   291	
   292	        private Task OnMaskedValueChangedAsync(string s) => SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(s);
   293	
   294	        private string GetCounterText() => Counter switch
   295	        {
   296	            null => string.Empty,
   297	            0 => string.IsNullOrEmpty(ReadText) ? "0" : $"{ReadText.Length}",
   298	            _ => (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ReadText) ? "0" : $"{ReadText.Length}") + $" / {Counter}"
   299	        };
   300	
   301	        protected async Task HandleContainerClickAsync()
   302	        {
   303	            if (!_isFocused && IsJSRuntimeAvailable && InputReference != null)
   304	            {
   305	                await InputReference.FocusAsync();
   306	            }
   307	        }
   308	    }

2026-05-29 15:37:19,065 - INFO - swea-agent-MudBlazor__MudBlazor-12958 - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

     1	﻿using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
     2	using MudBlazor.State;
     3	using MudBlazor.Utilities.Debounce;
     4	
     5	namespace MudBlazor
     6	{
     7	    /// <summary>
     8	    /// A base class for designing input components which update after a delay.
     9	    /// </summary>
    10	    /// <typeparam name="T">The type of object managed by this input.</typeparam>
    11	    public abstract class MudDebouncedInput<T> : MudBaseInput<T>
    12	    {
    13	        private DebounceDispatcher? _debouncer;
    14	
    15	        protected MudDebouncedInput()
    16	        {
    17	            using var registerScope = CreateRegisterScope();
    18	            registerScope.RegisterParameter<double>(nameof(DebounceInterval))
    19	                .WithParameter(() => DebounceInterval)
    20	                .WithComparer(DoubleEpsilonEqualityComparer.Default)
    21	                .WithChangeHandler(OnDebounceIntervalChangedAsync);
    22	        }
    23	
    24	        [Inject]
    25	        private TimeProvider TimeProvider { get; set; } = null!;
    26	
    27	        /// <summary>
    28	        /// The number of milliseconds to wait before updating the <see cref="MudBaseInput{T}.Text"/> value.
    29	        /// </summary>
    30	        [Parameter, ParameterState(ParameterUsage = ParameterUsageOptions.None)]
    31	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Behavior)]
    32	        public double DebounceInterval { get; set; }
    33	
    34	        /// <summary>
    35	        /// Occurs when the <see cref="DebounceInterval"/> has elapsed.
    36	        /// </summary>
    37	        /// <remarks>
    38	        /// The value in <see cref="MudBaseInput{T}.Text"/> is included in this event.
    39	        /// </remarks>
    40	        [Parameter]
    41	        public EventCallback<string> OnDebounceIntervalElapsed { get; set; }
    42	
    43	        /// <inheritdoc />
    44	        protected override Task UpdateTextPropertyAsync(bool updateValue)
    45	        {
    46	            // Don't update text if we're debouncing and the value hasn't actually changed
    47	            var suppressTextUpdate = !updateValue
    48	                                     && DebounceInterval > 0
    49	                                     && _debouncer is not null
    50	                                     && _debouncer.IsPending;
    51	
    52	            return suppressTextUpdate
    53	                ? Task.CompletedTask
    54	                : base.UpdateTextPropertyAsync(updateValue);
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        /// <inheritdoc />
    58	        protected override Task UpdateValuePropertyAsync(bool updateText)
    59	        {
    60	            // This method is called when Value property needs to be refreshed from the current Text property, so typically because Text property has changed.
    61	            // We want to debounce only text-input, not a value being set, so the debouncing is only done when updateText==false (because that indicates the
    62	            // change came from a Text setter)
    63	            if (updateText)
    64	            {
    65	                // we have a change coming not from the Text setter, no debouncing is needed
    66	                return base.UpdateValuePropertyAsync(updateText);
    67	            }
    68	            // if debounce interval is 0 or no debouncer, we update immediately
    69	            if (DebounceInterval <= 0 || _debouncer is null)
    70	            {
    71	                return base.UpdateValuePropertyAsync(updateText);
    72	            }
    73	
    74	            // Debounce the update - use fire-and-forget pattern to match the old Timer implementation.
    75	            _ = _debouncer.DebounceAsync(OnDebouncedUpdate);
    76	            return Task.CompletedTask;
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        /// <inheritdoc />
    80	        protected override async Task ValidateValue()
    81	        {
    82	            if (await SynchronizePendingValueForValidationAsync())
    83	            {
    84	                return;
    85	            }
    86	
    87	            await base.ValidateValue();
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        /// <inheritdoc />
    91	        protected override void OnParametersSet()
    92	        {
    93	            base.OnParametersSet();
    94	            // if input is to be debounced, makes sense to bind the change of the text to oninput
    95	            // so we set Immediate to true
    96	            if (DebounceInterval > 0)
    97	            {
    98	                // TODO: Don't write to parameter directly
    99	                Immediate = true;
   100	            }
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        private async Task OnDebounceIntervalChangedAsync(ParameterChangedEventArgs<double> args)
   104	        {
   105	            if (args.Value <= 0)
   106	            {
   107	                // not debounced, dispose debouncer if any
   108	                _debouncer?.Dispose();
   109	                _debouncer = null;
   110	                return;
   111	            }
   112	
   113	            // Create debouncer if we don't have one
   114	            if (_debouncer is null)
   115	            {
   116	                _debouncer = new DebounceDispatcher(TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(args.Value), false, TimeProvider);
   117	            }
   118	            else
   119	            {
   120	                // Only update interval if it has meaningfully changed
   121	                // Use DoubleEpsilonEqualityComparer to avoid unnecessary updates due to floating-point precision
   122	                if (!DoubleEpsilonEqualityComparer.Default.Equals(args.LastValue, args.Value))
   123	                {
   124	                    await _debouncer.UpdateIntervalAsync(TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(args.Value));
   125	                }
   126	            }
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        private async Task<bool> SynchronizePendingValueForValidationAsync()
   130	        {
   131	            if (DebounceInterval <= 0 || _debouncer is null || !_debouncer.IsPending)
   132	            {
   133	                return false;
   134	            }
   135	
   136	            var pendingValue = ConvertGet(ReadText);
   137	            var pendingValueChanged = !EqualityComparer<T?>.Default.Equals(ReadValue, pendingValue);
   138	
   139	            await _debouncer.CancelAsync();
   140	
   141	            if (!pendingValueChanged)
   142	            {
   143	                return false;
   144	            }
   145	
   146	            // SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync already triggers FieldChanged and BeginValidateAsync,
   147	            // so the synced validation happens there and this call can stop.
   148	            await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(pendingValue, updateText: false);
   149	            return true;
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        private Task OnDebouncedUpdate()
   153	        {
   154	            return InvokeAsync(async () =>
   155	            {
   156	                await base.UpdateValuePropertyAsync(false);
   157	                await OnDebounceIntervalElapsed.InvokeAsync(ReadText);
   158	            });
   159	        }
   160	
   161	        /// <inheritdoc />
   162	        protected override async ValueTask DisposeAsyncCore()
   163	        {
   164	            await base.DisposeAsyncCore();
   165	            _debouncer?.Dispose();
   166	            _debouncer = null;
   167	        }
   168	    }
   169	}

   270	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Behavior)]

   501	        /// <summary>
   502	        /// Displays the search result drop-down.
   503	        /// </summary>
   504	        /// <remarks>
   505	        /// When this property changes, the <see cref="OpenChanged"/> event will occur.
   506	        /// </remarks>
   507	        public bool Open
   508	        {
   509	            get => _open;
   510	            // Note: the setter is protected because it was needed by a user who derived his own autocomplete from this class.
   511	            // Note: setting Open will not open or close it. Use ToggleAsync() for that.
   512	            protected set
   513	            {
   514	                if (_open == value)
   515	                    return;
   516	                _open = value;
   517	
   518	                OpenChanged.InvokeAsync(_open).CatchAndLog();
   519	            }
   520	        }
   521	
   522	        private bool IsLoading => _currentSearchTask is { IsCompleted: false };
   523	
   524	        private string CurrentIcon
   525	        {
   526	            get
   527	            {
   528	                if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(AdornmentIcon))
   529	                {
   530	                    return AdornmentIcon;
   531	                }
   532	
   533	                return _open ? CloseIcon : OpenIcon;
   534	            }
   535	        }
   536	
   537	        /// <summary>
   538	        /// Returns a value for the <c>autocomplete</c> attribute, either supplied by default or the one specified in the attribute overrides.
   539	        /// </summary>
   540	        protected object? GetAutocomplete() => UserAttributes.GetValueOrDefault("autocomplete", "off");
   541	
   542	        public MudAutocomplete()
   543	        {
   544	            Adornment = Adornment.End;
   545	            IconSize = Size.Medium;
   546	            Immediate = true;
   547	        }
   548	
   549	        /// <summary>
   550	        /// Changes the currently selected item to the specified value.
   551	        /// </summary>
   552	        /// <param name="value">The value to set.</param>
   553	        public async Task SelectOptionAsync(T value)
   554	        {
   555	            _isProcessingValue = true;
   556	            try
   557	            {
   558	                // #1 needs to close before SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync so that whatever the user puts in ValueChanged can run without the popover being in front of it
   559	                // #2 Use "Open" field instead of property to prevent raising multiple OpenChanged events while selecting item.
   560	                _open = false;
   561	
   562	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(value);
   563	
   564	                // needs to be open to run the rest of the code
   565	                _open = true;
   566	
   567	                if (_items != null)
   568	                    _selectedListItemIndex = Array.IndexOf(_items, value);
   569	
   570	                var optionText = GetItemString(value);
   571	
   572	                if (!_isCleared)
   573	                    await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(optionText, false);
   574	
   575	                _debounceTimer?.Dispose();
   576	
   577	                await BeginValidateAsync();
   578	
   579	                if (!_isCleared)
   580	                {
   581	                    await _elementReference.SetText(optionText);
   582	                }
   583	
   584	                Open = false;
   585	                StateHasChanged();
   586	            }
   587	            finally
   588	            {
   589	                _isProcessingValue = false;
   590	            }
   591	        }
   592	
   593	        protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
   594	        {
   595	            await base.OnInitializedAsync();
   596	            var text = GetItemString(ReadValue);
   597	            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(text))
   598	            {
   599	                await SetTextCoreAsync(text);
   600	            }
   601	        }
   602	
   603	        protected override void OnAfterRender(bool firstRender)
   604	        {
   605	            if (_isClearing || _isProcessingValue)
   606	            {
   607	                //When you select a value in the popover, SelectOptionAsync will be called.
   608	                //When it reaches SetValueAsync, it will be awaited.
   609	                //Meanwhile, in parallel, the ClearAsync method will be called, which sets isCleared to true.
   610	                //However, by the time SetValueAsync is released and SelectOptionAsync continues its execution, an OnAfterRender event might fire, setting isCleared back to false.
   611	                //This can result in a race condition.
   612	                //https://github.com/MudBlazor/MudBlazor/pull/6701
   613	                base.OnAfterRender(firstRender);
   614	                return;
   615	            }
   616	
   617	            _isCleared = false;
   618	
   619	            base.OnAfterRender(firstRender);
   620	        }
   621	
   622	        protected override Task UpdateTextPropertyAsync(bool updateValue)
   623	        {
   624	            // This keeps the text from being set when ClearAsync() was called
   625	            if (_isCleared)
   626	                return Task.CompletedTask;
   627	
   628	            return base.UpdateTextPropertyAsync(updateValue);
   629	        }
   630	
   631	        protected override async Task UpdateValuePropertyAsync(bool updateText)
   632	        {
   633	            _debounceTimer?.Dispose();
   634	
   635	            if (ResetValueOnEmptyText && string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(ReadText))
   636	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(default(T), updateText);
   637	            else if (Immediate)
   638	                await CoerceValueToTextAsync();
   639	
   640	            if (DebounceInterval <= 0)
   641	                await OpenMenuAsync();
   642	            else
   643	                _debounceTimer = TimeProvider.CreateTimer(OnDebounceComplete, null, TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(DebounceInterval), Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan);
   644	        }
   645	
   646	        private void OnDebounceComplete(object? stateInfo) => InvokeAsync(OpenMenuAsync);
   647	
   648	        private void CancelToken()
   649	        {
   650	            try
   651	            {
   652	                _cancellationTokenSrc?.Cancel();
   653	            }
   654	            catch { /*ignored*/ }
   655	            finally
   656	            {
   657	                _cancellationTokenSrc = new CancellationTokenSource();
   658	            }
   659	        }
   660	
   661	        private Task SetReturnedItemsCountAsync(int value)
   662	        {
   663	            _returnedItemsCount = value;
   664	            return ReturnedItemsCountChanged.InvokeAsync(value);
   665	        }
   666	
   667	        /// <summary>
   668	        /// Opens or closes the drop-down of items depending on whether it was closed or open.
   669	        /// </summary>
   670	        /// <remarks>
   671	        /// Will have no effect if the autocomplete is disabled or read-only.
   672	        /// </remarks>
   673	        public Task ToggleMenuAsync()
   674	        {
   675	            if (!Open && (GetDisabledState() || GetReadOnlyState()))
   676	            {
   677	                return Task.CompletedTask;
   678	            }
   679	
   680	            return Open ? CloseMenuAsync() : OpenMenuAsync();
   681	        }
   682	
   683	        /// <summary>
   684	        /// Closes the drop-down of items.
   685	        /// </summary>
   686	        public async Task CloseMenuAsync()
   687	        {
   688	            CancelToken();
   689	            _debounceTimer?.Dispose();
   690	            Open = false; // Before restoring position and triggering changes, make sure that we close the popover
   691	            StateHasChanged();
   692	            await RestoreScrollPositionAsync();
   693	            await CoerceTextToValueAsync();
   694	        }
   695	
   696	        /// <summary>
   697	        /// Opens the drop-down of items, or refreshes the list if it is already open.
   698	        /// </summary>
   699	        public async Task OpenMenuAsync()
   700	        {
   701	            if (MinCharacters > 0 && (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(ReadText) || ReadText.Length < MinCharacters))
   702	            {
   703	                Open = false;
   704	                StateHasChanged();
   705	                return;
   706	            }
   707	
   708	            _opening = true;
   709	
   710	            var searchedItems = Array.Empty<T>();
   711	            CancelToken();
   712	
   713	            var wasFocused = _isFocused;
   714	            var searchingWhileSelected = false;
   715	            try
   716	            {
   717	                if (ProgressIndicatorInPopoverTemplate != null)
   718	                {
   719	                    // Open before searching if a progress indicator is defined.
   720	                    Open = true;
   721	                }
   722	
   723	                // Search while selected if enabled and the Text is equivalent to the Value.
   724	                searchingWhileSelected = !_isValueCoerced && !Strict && ReadValue != null && (ReadValue!.ToString() == ReadText || (ToStringFunc != null && ToStringFunc(ReadValue!) == ReadText));
   725	                _cancellationTokenSrc ??= new CancellationTokenSource();
   726	                var searchText = searchingWhileSelected ? string.Empty : ReadText;
   727	                var searchTask = SearchFunc?.Invoke(searchText, _cancellationTokenSrc.Token);
   728	
   729	                _currentSearchTask = searchTask;
   730	
   731	                StateHasChanged();
   732	                searchedItems = searchTask switch
   733	                {
   734	                    null => [],
   735	                    _ => (await searchTask).ToArray()
   736	                };
   737	            }
   738	            catch (TaskCanceledException)
   739	            {
   740	            }
   741	            catch (OperationCanceledException)
   742	            {
   743	            }
   744	            catch (Exception e)
   745	            {
   746	                Logger.LogWarning("The search function failed to return results: " + e.Message);
   747	            }
   748	
   749	            await SetReturnedItemsCountAsync(searchedItems.Length);
   750	
   751	            if (MaxItems.HasValue)
   752	            {
   753	                int startIndex = 0;
   754	                int length = Math.Min(MaxItems.Value, searchedItems.Length);
   755	
   756	                // Get range of items based off selected item so the selected item can be scrolled to when strict is set to false
   757	                if (!Strict && searchedItems.Length != 0 && !EqualityComparer<T>.Default.Equals(ReadValue, default(T)))
   758	                {
   759	                    int maxItems = MaxItems.Value;
   760	                    int valueIndex = Array.IndexOf(searchedItems, ReadValue);
   761	
   762	                    // Center the selected item in the list if possible
   763	                    int half = maxItems / 2;
   764	                    startIndex = valueIndex - half;
   765	                    int endIndex = startIndex + maxItems;
   766	
   767	                    // Adjust if out of bounds
   768	                    if (startIndex < 0)
   769	                    {
   770	                        startIndex = 0;
   771	                        endIndex = Math.Min(maxItems, searchedItems.Length);
   772	                    }
   773	                    else if (endIndex > searchedItems.Length)
   774	                    {
   775	                        endIndex = searchedItems.Length;
   776	                        startIndex = Math.Max(0, endIndex - maxItems);
   777	                    }
   778	
   779	                    length = endIndex - startIndex;
   780	                }
   781	
   782	                if (length < searchedItems.Length)
   783	                {
   784	                    var slicedItems = new T[length];
   785	                    Array.Copy(searchedItems, startIndex, slicedItems, 0, length);
   786	                    searchedItems = slicedItems;
   787	                }
   788	            }
   789	
   790	            _items = searchedItems;
   791	
   792	            var enabledItemIndices = new List<int>(_items.Length);
   793	            for (int i = 0; i < _items.Length; i++)
   794	            {
   795	                if (ItemDisabledFunc?.Invoke(_items[i]) != true)
   796	                {
   797	                    enabledItemIndices.Add(i);
   798	                }
   799	            }
   800	
   801	            _enabledItemIndices = enabledItemIndices;
   802	            if (searchingWhileSelected) //compute the index of the currently select value, if it exists
   803	            {
   804	                _selectedListItemIndex = Array.IndexOf(_items, ReadValue);
   805	            }
   806	            else
   807	            {
   808	                _selectedListItemIndex = _enabledItemIndices.Any() ? _enabledItemIndices[0] : -1;
   809	            }
   810	
   811	            if (_isFocused || !wasFocused)
   812	            {
   813	                // Open after the search has finished if we're still focused (UI), or were never focused in the first place (programmatically).
   814	                Open = true;
   815	            }
   816	
   817	            _opening = false;
   818	            StateHasChanged();
   819	
   820	            // If not strict scroll to the selected item
   821	            if (!Strict && _selectedListItemIndex > 0)
   822	            {
   823	                await ScrollToListItemAsync(_selectedListItemIndex);
   824	            }
   825	        }
   826	
   827	        protected override Task SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(T? value, bool updateText = true, bool force = false)
   828	        {
   829	            _isValueCoerced = false;
   830	            return base.SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(value, updateText, force);
   831	        }
   832	
   833	        /// <summary>
   834	        /// Resets the Text and Value, and closes the drop-down if it is open.
   835	        /// </summary>
   836	        public async Task ClearAsync()
   837	        {
   838	            _isClearing = true;
   839	            try
   840	            {
   841	                _isCleared = true;
   842	                Open = false;
   843	
   844	                await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(string.Empty, updateValue: false);
   845	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(default, updateText: false);
   846	
   847	                await _elementReference.ResetAsync();
   848	
   849	                _debounceTimer?.Dispose();
   850	                StateHasChanged();
   851	            }
   852	            finally
   853	            {
   854	                _isClearing = false;
   855	            }
   856	        }
   857	
   858	        protected override Task ResetValueAsync() => ClearAsync();
   859	
   860	        private string? GetItemString(T? item)
   861	        {
   862	            if (item is null)
   863	            {
   864	                return string.Empty;
   865	            }
   866	
   867	            try
   868	            {
   869	                return ConvertSet(item);
   870	            }
   871	            catch (NullReferenceException)
   872	            {
   873	                // ignore
   874	            }
   875	
   876	            return "null";
   877	        }
   878	
   879	        private async Task OnInputKeyDownAsync(KeyboardEventArgs args)
   880	        {
   881	            switch (args.Key)
   882	            {
   883	                // We need to catch Tab here because a tab will move focus to the next element and thus we'd never get the tab key in OnInputKeyUpAsync.
   884	                case "Tab":
   885	                    if (Open)
   886	                    {
   887	                        if (SelectValueOnTab)
   888	                            await OnEnterKeyAsync();
   889	                    }
   890	                    await CloseMenuAsync();
   891	                    break;
   892	                case "ArrowDown":
   893	                    if (Open)
   894	                    {
   895	                        await SelectAdjacentItemAsync(+1);
   896	                    }
   897	                    else
   898	                    {
   899	                        await OpenMenuAsync();
   900	                    }
   901	                    break;
   902	                case "ArrowUp":
   903	                    if (args.AltKey)
   904	                    {
   905	                        await CloseMenuAsync();
   906	                    }
   907	                    else if (!Open)
   908	                    {
   909	                        await OpenMenuAsync();
   910	                    }
   911	                    else
   912	                    {
   913	                        await SelectAdjacentItemAsync(-1);
   914	                    }
   915	                    break;
   916	            }
   917	
   918	            await base.InvokeKeyDownAsync(args);
   919	        }
   920	
   921	        private async Task OnInputKeyUpAsync(KeyboardEventArgs args)
   922	        {
   923	            switch (args.Key)
   924	            {
   925	                case "Enter":
   926	                case "NumpadEnter":
   927	                    if (Open)
   928	                    {
   929	                        await OnEnterKeyAsync();
   930	                    }
   931	                    else
   932	                    {
   933	                        await OpenMenuAsync();
   934	                    }
   935	                    break;
   936	                case "Escape":
   937	                    await CloseMenuAsync();
   938	                    break;
   939	                case "Backspace":
   940	                    if (args.CtrlKey && args.ShiftKey)
   941	                    {
   942	                        await ResetAsync();
   943	                    }
   944	                    break;
   945	            }
   946	
   947	            await base.InvokeKeyUpAsync(args);
   948	        }
   949	
   950	        /// <summary>
   951	        /// Selects the next or previous enabled item in the list and scrolls to it.
   952	        /// </summary>
   953	        /// <param name="direction">The direction to move, positive for down, negative for up.</param>
   954	        private ValueTask SelectAdjacentItemAsync(int direction)
   955	        {
   956	            if (_items == null || _items.Length == 0 || !_enabledItemIndices.Any())
   957	                return ValueTask.CompletedTask;
   958	
   959	            // Get the current index among enabled items
   960	            var currentEnabledIndex = _enabledItemIndices.IndexOf(_selectedListItemIndex);
   961	
   962	            // Determine the new index based on the direction
   963	            var newEnabledIndex = currentEnabledIndex + direction;
   964	
   965	            // Ensure new index is within bounds
   966	            if (newEnabledIndex >= 0 && newEnabledIndex < _enabledItemIndices.Count)
   967	            {
   968	                _selectedListItemIndex = _enabledItemIndices[newEnabledIndex];
   969	                return SelectItemAsync(_selectedListItemIndex);
   970	            }
   971	
   972	            return ValueTask.CompletedTask;
   973	        }
   974	
   975	        /// <summary>
   976	        /// Selects the item in the list at the specified index and scrolls to it.
   977	        /// </summary>
   978	        /// <param name="index">The index of the item to scroll to. If it's out of range then nothing will happen.</param>
   979	        private ValueTask SelectItemAsync(int index)
   980	        {
   981	            if (_items == null || _items.Length == 0 || !_enabledItemIndices.Any() || index < 0 || index > _enabledItemIndices.Count - 1)
   982	                return ValueTask.CompletedTask;
   983	
   984	            _selectedListItemIndex = index;
   985	
   986	            return ScrollToListItemAsync(index);
   987	        }
   988	
   989	        /// <summary>
   990	        /// Scrolls the list of items to the item at the specified index.
   991	        /// </summary>
   992	        /// <param name="index">The index of the item to scroll to.</param>
   993	        public ValueTask ScrollToListItemAsync(int index)
   994	        {
   995	            var id = GetListItemId(index);
   996	
   997	            //id of the scrolled element
   998	            return ScrollManager.ScrollToListItemAsync(id);
   999	        }
  1000	
  1001	        /// <summary>
  1002	        /// This restores the scroll position after closing the menu and element being 0
  1003	        /// </summary>
  1004	        private ValueTask RestoreScrollPositionAsync()
  1005	        {
  1006	            if (_selectedListItemIndex != 0)
  1007	                return ValueTask.CompletedTask;
  1008	
  1009	            return ScrollManager.ScrollToListItemAsync(GetListItemId(0));
  1010	        }
  1011	
  1012	        private string GetListItemId(in int index)
  1013	        {
  1014	            return $"{_componentId}_item{index}";
  1015	        }
  1016	
  1017	        internal async Task OnEnterKeyAsync()
  1018	        {
  1019	            if (!Open || _items == null || _items.Length == 0)
  1020	            {
  1021	                // When Immediate is enabled, then the CoerceValue is set by TextChanged
  1022	                // So only coerce the value on enter when Immediate is disabled
  1023	                if (!Immediate)
  1024	                {
  1025	                    await CoerceValueToTextAsync();
  1026	                }
  1027	                return;
  1028	            }
  1029	
  1030	            try
  1031	            {
  1032	                if (_selectedListItemIndex >= 0 && _selectedListItemIndex < _items.Length)
  1033	                    await SelectOptionAsync(_items[_selectedListItemIndex]);
  1034	            }
  1035	            finally
  1036	            {
  1037	                if (Open)
  1038	                    Open = false;
  1039	            }
  1040	        }
  1041	
  1042	        private Task OnInputClickedAsync()
  1043	        {
  1044	            if (GetDisabledState())
  1045	            {
  1046	                return Task.CompletedTask;
  1047	            }
  1048	
  1049	            return OnInputActivatedAsync(true);
  1050	        }
  1051	
  1052	        private async Task OnInputFocusedAsync()
  1053	        {
  1054	            if (GetDisabledState())
  1055	            {
  1056	                // This shouldn't be possible through the UI, but could be triggered in code.
  1057	                return;
  1058	            }
  1059	
  1060	            if (GetReadOnlyState())
  1061	            {
  1062	                // A readonly input doesn't trigger onblur later correctly, so we have to disable focus features for it.
  1063	                return;
  1064	            }
  1065	
  1066	            var wasFocused = _isFocused;
  1067	            _isFocused = true;
  1068	
  1069	            // Skip features that are not meant for internal focus events.
  1070	            if (_handleNextFocus)
  1071	            {
  1072	                _handleNextFocus = false;
  1073	                return;
  1074	            }
  1075	
  1076	            // Select the input text unless we're already focused or it will interfere with cursor selection.
  1077	            if (!wasFocused && SelectOnActivation)
  1078	            {
  1079	                await SelectAsync();
  1080	            }
  1081	
  1082	            await OnInputActivatedAsync(OpenOnFocus);
  1083	        }
  1084	
  1085	        private async Task OnInputActivatedAsync(bool openMenu)
  1086	        {
  1087	            // The click event also triggers the focus event so we don't want to unnecessarily handle both.
  1088	            if (openMenu && !Open && !_opening && !GetReadOnlyState())
  1089	            {
  1090	                await OpenMenuAsync();
  1091	            }
  1092	        }
  1093	
  1094	        internal async Task HandleClearButtonAsync(MouseEventArgs e)
  1095	        {
  1096	            // clear button clicked, let's make sure text is cleared and the menu has focus
  1097	
  1098	            // These lines prevent the menu from opening when OpenOnFocus is true, which is the default.
  1099	            _debounceTimer?.Dispose();
  1100	            if (_items?.Length > 0)
  1101	                _items = [];
  1102	            _open = true;
  1103	            await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(default, false);
  1104	            await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(null, false);
  1105	            _selectedListItemIndex = 0;
  1106	            StateHasChanged();
  1107	            await OnClearButtonClick.InvokeAsync(e);
  1108	            await BeginValidateAsync();
  1109	        }
  1110	        internal async Task AdornmentClickHandlerAsync()
  1111	        {
  1112	            if (OnAdornmentClick.HasDelegate)
  1113	            {
  1114	
  1115	                await OnAdornmentClick.InvokeAsync();
  1116	            }
  1117	            else
  1118	            {
  1119	                await ToggleMenuAsync();
  1120	                if (Open)
  1121	                    await FocusAsync();
  1122	            }
  1123	        }
  1124	
  1125	        private Task OnInputBlurredAsync(FocusEventArgs args)
  1126	        {
  1127	            _isFocused = false;
  1128	            _handleNextFocus = false;
  1129	
  1130	            // When Immediate is enabled, then the CoerceValue is set by TextChanged
  1131	            // So only coerce the value on blur when Immediate is disabled
  1132	            if (!Immediate)
  1133	            {
  1134	                return CoerceValueToTextAsync();
  1135	            }
  1136	
  1137	            return OnBlur.InvokeAsync(args);
  1138	            // we should not validate on blur in autocomplete, because the user needs to click out of the input to select a value,
  1139	            // resulting in a premature validation. thus, don't call base
  1140	            //base.OnBlurred(args);
  1141	        }
  1142	
  1143	        private Task OnOverlayClosedAsync()
  1144	        {
  1145	            if (Open)
  1146	            {
  1147	                return CloseMenuAsync();
  1148	            }
  1149	
  1150	            return Task.CompletedTask;
  1151	        }
  1152	
  1153	        private Task CoerceTextToValueAsync()
  1154	        {
  1155	            if (!CoerceText)
  1156	                return Task.CompletedTask;
  1157	
  1158	            if (ResetValueOnEmptyText && string.IsNullOrEmpty(ReadText))
  1159	                return Task.CompletedTask;
  1160	
  1161	            _debounceTimer?.Dispose();
  1162	
  1163	            var text = ReadValue == null ? null : GetItemString(ReadValue);
  1164	
  1165	            // Don't update the value to prevent the popover from opening again after coercion
  1166	            if (text != ReadText)
  1167	                return SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(text, updateValue: false);
  1168	
  1169	            return Task.CompletedTask;
  1170	        }
  1171	
  1172	        private async Task CoerceValueToTextAsync()
  1173	        {
  1174	            if (!CoerceValue)
  1175	                return;
  1176	
  1177	            _debounceTimer?.Dispose();
  1178	
  1179	            var value = ConvertGet(ReadText);
  1180	            await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(value, updateText: false);
  1181	
  1182	            // We must set _isValueCoerced to true after calling SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync, as it sets it to false
  1183	            // CoerceValue is always true at this point, so we can set the value to true rather than checking the property again
  1184	            _isValueCoerced = true;
  1185	        }
  1186	
  1187	        /// <remarks>
  1188	        /// If <see cref="ToStringFunc"/> is set, it is used to convert the value to a string; otherwise, the base implementation is used.
  1189	        /// </remarks>
  1190	        /// <inheritdoc />
  1191	        protected override string? ConvertSet(T? input)
  1192	        {
  1193	            return ToStringFunc is not null
  1194	                ? ToStringFunc(input)
  1195	                : base.ConvertSet(input);
  1196	        }
  1197	
  1198	        /// <inheritdoc />
  1199	        protected override async ValueTask DisposeAsyncCore()
  1200	        {
  1201	            if (_debounceTimer is not null)
  1202	            {
  1203	                await _debounceTimer.DisposeAsync();
  1204	            }
  1205	
  1206	            if (_cancellationTokenSrc is not null)
  1207	            {
  1208	                try
  1209	                {
  1210	                    await _cancellationTokenSrc.CancelAsync();
  1211	                }
  1212	                catch { /*ignored*/ }
  1213	                try
  1214	                {
  1215	                    _cancellationTokenSrc.Dispose();
  1216	                }
  1217	                catch { /*ignored*/ }
  1218	            }
  1219	
  1220	            await base.DisposeAsyncCore();
  1221	        }
  1222	
  1223	        /// <summary>
  1224	        /// Sets focus to this Autocomplete.
  1225	        /// </summary>
  1226	        public override ValueTask FocusAsync()
  1227	        {
  1228	            return _elementReference.FocusAsync();
  1229	        }
  1230	
  1231	        /// <summary>
  1232	        /// Releases focus from this Autocomplete.
  1233	        /// </summary>

  1237	        }
  1238	
  1239	        /// <summary>
  1240	        /// Selects all the current text within the Autocomplete text box.
  1241	        /// </summary>
  1242	        public override ValueTask SelectAsync()
  1243	        {

  1245	        }
  1246	
  1247	        /// <summary>
  1248	        /// Selects a portion of the text within the Autocomplete text box.
  1249	        /// </summary>

  1251	        /// <param name="pos2">The index of the last character to select.</param>
  1252	        /// <returns>A <see cref="ValueTask"/> object.</returns>
  1253	        public override ValueTask SelectRangeAsync(int pos1, int pos2)
  1254	        {
  1255	            return _elementReference.SelectRangeAsync(pos1, pos2);
  1256	        }
  1257	
  1258	        private async Task OnTextChangedAsync(string? text)
  1259	        {
  1260	            if (text == null)
  1261	                return;
  1262	
  1263	            await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(text, true);
  1264	        }
  1265	
  1266	        private async Task ListItemOnClickAsync(T item)
  1267	        {
  1268	            _handleNextFocus = true; // Let the event handler know it doesn't need to do anything.
  1269	            await FocusAsync();
  1270	
  1271	            await SelectOptionAsync(item);
  1272	        }
  1273	    }

   133	        private bool IsNumberMode => InputMode == InputMode.numeric || InputMode == InputMode.@decimal;

   135	        // Defensive null check with object pattern: GetCulture() is annotated as non-null, but DataGrid may return null in certain cases.

   139	            Pattern is not null ||
   140	            GetFormat() is not null ||
   141	            // Edgy way to check if the MudComponentForm.Culture is provided explicitly and is a different one than the default CurrentUICulture && InvariantCulture.
   142	            // If not, then we override to InvariantCulture to avoid issues with <input type="number">.
   143	            (GetCulture() is { } culture && !culture.Equals(CultureInfo.CurrentUICulture) && !culture.Equals(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture));
   144	
   145	        /// <inheritdoc />
   146	        [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
   147	        public override ValueTask FocusAsync()
   148	        {
   149	            return _elementReference.FocusAsync();
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        /// <inheritdoc />
   153	        [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
   154	        public override ValueTask BlurAsync()
   155	        {
   156	            return _elementReference.BlurAsync();
   157	        }
   158	
   159	        /// <inheritdoc />
   160	        [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
   161	        public override ValueTask SelectAsync()
   162	        {
   163	            return _elementReference.SelectAsync();
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        /// <inheritdoc />
   167	        [ExcludeFromCodeCoverage]
   168	        public override ValueTask SelectRangeAsync(int pos1, int pos2)
   169	        {
   170	            return _elementReference.SelectRangeAsync(pos1, pos2);
   171	        }
   172	
   173	        /// <inheritdoc />
   174	        protected override Task SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(T? value, bool updateText = true, bool force = false)
   175	        {
   176	            (value, var valueChanged) = ConstrainBoundaries(value);
   177	            return base.SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(value, valueChanged || updateText, force);
   178	        }
   179	
   180	        /// <inheritdoc />
   181	        protected internal override async Task OnBlurredAsync(FocusEventArgs obj)
   182	        {
   183	            await base.OnBlurredAsync(obj);
   184	
   185	            if (Immediate || DebounceInterval > 0)
   186	            {
   187	                await UpdateValuePropertyAsync(true); //Required to set the value after a blur before the debounce period has elapsed
   188	            }
   189	            else
   190	            {
   191	                // For non-immediate, non-debounced inputs, browser onchange timing can race with blur handlers.
   192	                // Parse current text only when it is not already the formatted representation of the current value.
   193	                var formattedValueText = ConvertSet(ReadValue);
   194	                if (!string.Equals(ReadText, formattedValueText, StringComparison.Ordinal))
   195	                {
   196	                    await UpdateValuePropertyAsync(true);
   197	                }
   198	            }
   199	
   200	            await UpdateTextPropertyAsync(false); //Required to update the string formatting after a blur before the debounce period has elapsed
   201	
   202	            if (IsFormatted && DebounceInterval <= 0 && !ConversionError)
   203	            {
   204	                await _elementReference.SetText(ReadText, updateValue: false);
   205	            }
   206	        }
   207	
   208	        protected async Task<bool> ValidateInput(T? value)
   209	        {
   210	            (value, var valueChanged) = ConstrainBoundaries(value);
   211	            if (valueChanged)
   212	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(value, true);
   213	            return true; //Don't show errors
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        /// <summary>
   217	        /// Shows a button to clear the value.
   218	        /// </summary>
   219	        [Parameter]
   220	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Behavior)]
   221	        public bool Clearable { get; set; } = false;
   222	
   223	        /// <summary>
   224	        /// The icon of the clear button when <see cref="Clearable"/> is <c>true</c>.
   225	        /// </summary>
   226	        /// <remarks>
   227	        /// Defaults to <see cref="Icons.Material.Filled.Clear"/>.
   228	        /// </remarks>
   229	        [Parameter]
   230	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Appearance)]
   231	        public string ClearIcon { get; set; } = Icons.Material.Filled.Clear;
   232	
   233	        /// <summary>
   234	        /// Decrements or increments depending on factor
   235	        /// </summary>
   236	        /// <param name="factor">Multiplication factor (1 or -1) will be applied to the step</param>
   237	        private async Task Change(double factor = 1)
   238	        {
   239	            try
   240	            {
   241	                var nextValue = GetNextValue(factor) ?? Num.To<T>(0);
   242	
   243	                // validate that the data type is a value type before we compare them
   244	                if (typeof(T).IsValueType && ReadValue is not null)
   245	                {
   246	                    if (factor > 0 && _comparer.Compare(nextValue, ReadValue) < 0)
   247	                        nextValue = Max;
   248	                    else if (factor < 0 && _comparer.Compare(nextValue, ReadValue) > 0)
   249	                        nextValue = Min;
   250	                }
   251	
   252	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(ConstrainBoundaries(nextValue).value);
   253	                await _elementReference.SetText(ReadText);
   254	            }
   255	            catch (OverflowException)
   256	            {
   257	                // if next value overflows the primitive type, lets set it to Min or Max depending on if factor is positive or negative
   258	                await SetValueAndUpdateTextAsync(factor > 0 ? Max : Min, true);
   259	            }
   260	        }
   261	
   262	        private T? GetNextValue(double factor)
   263	        {
   264	            if (typeof(T) == typeof(decimal) || typeof(T) == typeof(decimal?))
   265	                return (T)(object)Convert.ToDecimal(FromDecimal(ReadValue) + (FromDecimal(Step) * (decimal)factor));
   266	            if (typeof(T) == typeof(long) || typeof(T) == typeof(long?))
   267	                return (T)(object)Convert.ToInt64(FromInt64(ReadValue) + (FromInt64(Step) * factor));
   268	            if (typeof(T) == typeof(ulong) || typeof(T) == typeof(ulong?))
   269	                return (T)(object)Convert.ToUInt64(FromUInt64(ReadValue) + (FromUInt64(Step) * factor));
   270	            return Num.To<T>(Num.From(ReadValue) + (Num.From(Step) * factor));
   271	        }
   272	
   273	        /// <summary>
   274	        /// Increases the current value by <see cref="Step"/>.
   275	        /// </summary>
   276	        public Task Increment() => Change(factor: 1);
   277	
   278	        /// <summary>
   279	        /// Decreases the current value by <see cref="Step"/>.
   280	        /// </summary>
   281	        public Task Decrement() => Change(factor: -1);
   282	
   283	        /// <summary>
   284	        /// Checks if the value respects the boundaries set for this instance.
   285	        /// </summary>
   286	        /// <param name="value">Value to check.</param>
   287	        /// <returns>Returns a valid value and if it has been changed.</returns>
   288	        protected (T? value, bool changed) ConstrainBoundaries(T? value)
   289	        {
   290	            if (value == null)
   291	                return (default(T), false);
   292	
   293	            // validate that the data type is a value type before we compare them
   294	            if (typeof(T).IsValueType)
   295	            {
   296	                // check if value is bigger than defined MAX, if so take the defined MAX value instead
   297	                if (_comparer.Compare(value, Max) > 0)
   298	                    return (Max, true);
   299	
   300	                // check if value is lower than defined MIN, if so take the defined MIN value instead
   301	                if (_comparer.Compare(value, Min) < 0)
   302	                    return (Min, true);
   303	            }
   304	
   305	            return (value, false);
   306	        }
   307	
   308	        protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
   309	        {
   310	            if (firstRender)
   311	            {
   312	                var keyOptions = new List<KeyOptions>
   313	                {
   314	                    // prevent scrolling page, instead increment
   315	                    new("ArrowUp", preventDown: "key+none"),
   316	                    // prevent scrolling page, instead decrement
   317	                    new("ArrowDown", preventDown: "key+none"),
   318	                     // prevent dead keys like ^ ` ´ etc
   319	                    new("Dead", preventDown: "key+any"),
   320	                };
   321	
   322	                if (Pattern != null)
   323	                {
   324	                    //prevent inputs that do not match the pattern
   325	                    keyOptions.Add(new($"/^(?!{Pattern.TrimEnd('*')}).$/", preventDown: "key+none|key+shift|key+alt"));
   326	                }
   327	
   328	                var options = new KeyInterceptorOptions("mud-input-slot", keyOptions.ToArray());
   329	
   330	                await KeyInterceptorService.SubscribeAsync(_elementId, options, keys => keys
   331	                    .When(CanHandleKeys, builder => builder
   332	                        .OnKeyDown("ArrowUp", Increment)
   333	                        .OnKeyDown("ArrowDown", Decrement)));
   334	            }
   335	
   336	            await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);
   337	
   338	            if (!firstRender)
   339	            {
   340	                return;
   341	            }
   342	
   343	            // Overrides the browser's culture since <input type="number"> does not consider culture.
   344	            // If a specific Culture, Pattern, or Format is defined, <input type="text"> will be used 
   345	            // with the corresponding attributes applied.
   346	            if (!IsFormatted)
   347	            {
   348	                await SetCultureAsync(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
   349	            }
   350	        }
   351	
   352	        private bool CanHandleKeys() => !GetDisabledState() && !GetReadOnlyState();
   353	
   354	        protected async Task HandleKeyDownAsync(KeyboardEventArgs obj)
   355	        {
   356	            await KeyInterceptorService.DispatchAsync(_elementId, KeyEventKind.Down, obj);
   357	            await OnKeyDown.InvokeAsync(obj);
   358	        }
   359	
   360	        protected Task HandleKeyUpAsync(KeyboardEventArgs obj)
   361	        {
   362	            if (GetDisabledState() || GetReadOnlyState())
   363	                return Task.CompletedTask;
   364	
   365	            return OnKeyUp.InvokeAsync(obj);
   366	        }
   367	
   368	        protected async Task OnMouseWheelAsync(WheelEventArgs obj)
   369	        {
   370	            if (!obj.ShiftKey || GetDisabledState() || GetReadOnlyState())
   371	                return;
   372	            if (obj.DeltaY < 0)
   373	            {
   374	                if (InvertMouseWheel == false)
   375	                    await Increment();
   376	                else
   377	                    await Decrement();
   378	            }
   379	            else if (obj.DeltaY > 0)
   380	            {
   381	                if (InvertMouseWheel == false)
   382	                    await Decrement();
   383	                else
   384	                    await Increment();
   385	            }
   386	        }
   387	
   388	        /// <summary>
   389	        /// Reverses the mouse wheel direction.
   390	        /// </summary>
   391	        /// <remarks>
   392	        /// Defaults to <c>false</c>.  
   393	        /// When <c>true</c>, moving the mouse wheel up will decrease the value, and down will increase the value.
   394	        /// </remarks>
   395	        [Parameter]
   396	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Behavior)]
   397	        public bool InvertMouseWheel { get; set; } = false;
   398	
   399	        /// <summary>
   400	        /// The minimum allowed value.
   401	        /// </summary>
   402	        /// <remarks>
   403	        /// Defaults to the minimum value of the numeric type, such as <see cref="int.MinValue"/>.
   404	        /// </remarks>
   405	        [Parameter]
   406	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Validation)]
   407	        public T? Min
   408	        {
   409	            get => _minHasValue ? _min : _minDefault;
   410	            set
   411	            {
   412	                _minHasValue = value != null;
   413	                _min = value;
   414	            }
   415	        }
   416	
   417	        /// <summary>
   418	        /// The maximum allowed value.
   419	        /// </summary>
   420	        /// <remarks>
   421	        /// Defaults to the maximum value of the numeric type, such as <see cref="int.MaxValue"/>.
   422	        /// </remarks>
   423	        [Parameter]
   424	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Validation)]
   425	        public T? Max
   426	        {
   427	            get => _maxHasValue ? _max : _maxDefault;
   428	            set
   429	            {
   430	                _maxHasValue = value != null;
   431	                _max = value;
   432	            }
   433	        }
   434	
   435	        /// <summary>
   436	        /// The amount added or subtracted when changing values.
   437	        /// </summary>
   438	        /// <remarks>
   439	        /// Defaults to <c>1</c>.  
   440	        /// This affects changing values via spin buttons or the keyboard.
   441	        /// </remarks>
   442	        [Parameter]
   443	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Behavior)]
   444	        public T? Step
   445	        {
   446	            get => _stepHasValue ? _step : _stepDefault;
   447	            set
   448	            {
   449	                _stepHasValue = value != null;
   450	                _step = value;
   451	            }
   452	        }
   453	
   454	        /// <summary>
   455	        /// Hides the up and down buttons.
   456	        /// </summary>
   457	        /// <remarks>
   458	        /// Defaults to <c>false</c>.  When <c>false</c>, the user can still change values with the keyboard arrows and by typing values.
   459	        /// </remarks>
   460	        [Parameter]
   461	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Appearance)]
   462	        public bool HideSpinButtons { get; set; }
   463	
   464	        /// <summary>
   465	        /// The type of value collected by this field.
   466	        /// </summary>
   467	        /// <remarks>
   468	        /// Defaults to <see cref="InputMode.numeric"/>.
   469	        /// </remarks>
   470	        [Parameter]
   471	        public override InputMode InputMode { get; set; } = InputMode.numeric;
   472	
   473	        /// <summary>
   474	        /// The regular expression used to constrain values.
   475	        /// </summary>
   476	        /// <remarks>
   477	        /// Defaults to <c>null</c>, which will show a numerical keyboard on Safari.  Must be a valid JavaScript regular expression.  To allow only numbers (with no signs or commas), you can use <c>[0-9.]</c>.
   478	        /// </remarks>
   479	        [Parameter]
   480	        public override string? Pattern { get; set; } = null;
   481	
   482	        private string GetCounterText() => Counter switch
   483	        {
   484	            null => string.Empty,
   485	            0 => string.IsNullOrEmpty(ReadText) ? "0" : $"{ReadText.Length}",
   486	            _ => (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ReadText) ? "0" : $"{ReadText.Length}") + $" / {Counter}"
   487	        };
   488	
   489	        private async Task OnInputValueChanged(string text)
   490	        {
   491	            await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(text);
   492	
   493	            // Keep formatted text in sync when using formatted input mode.
   494	            // This also covers onchange updates that can occur around blur timing.
   495	            if (IsFormatted && DebounceInterval <= 0 && !ConversionError)
   496	            {
   497	                var formattedText = ConvertSet(ReadValue);
   498	                if (!string.Equals(ReadText, formattedText, StringComparison.Ordinal))
   499	                {
   500	                    await SetTextCoreAsync(formattedText);
   501	                    await _elementReference.SetText(formattedText, updateValue: false);
   502	                }
   503	            }
   504	        }
   505	
   506	        //avoids the format to use scientific notation for large or small number in floating points types, while covering all options
   507	        //https://stackoverflow.com/questions/1546113/double-to-string-conversion-without-scientific-notation
   508	        private const string TagFormat = "0.###################################################################################################################################################################################################################################################################################################################################################";
   509	
   510	        private static string? FormatParam(T? value)
   511	        {
   512	            if (value is IFormattable f)
   513	                return f.ToString(TagFormat, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture.NumberFormat);
   514	            return null;
   515	        }
   516	
   517	        private static decimal FromDecimal(T? v) => Convert.ToDecimal((decimal?)(object?)v);
   518	
   519	        private static long FromInt64(T? v) => Convert.ToInt64((long?)(object?)v);
   520	
   521	        private static ulong FromUInt64(T? v) => Convert.ToUInt64((ulong?)(object?)v);
   522	
   523	        /// <inheritdoc />
   524	        protected override async ValueTask DisposeAsyncCore()
   525	        {
   526	            await base.DisposeAsyncCore();
   527	
   528	            if (IsJSRuntimeAvailable)
   529	            {
   530	                await KeyInterceptorService.UnsubscribeAsync(_elementId);
   531	            }
   532	        }
   533	    }
   534	}

    16	/// <summary>
    17	/// Represents a base class for radial charts.
    18	/// </summary>
    19	/// <typeparam name="T">The data type of the chart.</typeparam>
    20	/// <typeparam name="TOptions">The type of options for the chart.</typeparam>
    21	public abstract class MudRadialChartBase<T, TOptions> : MudChartBase<T, TOptions>, IDisposable
    22	    where T : struct, INumber<T>, IMinMaxValue<T>, IFormattable
    23	    where TOptions : IRadialChartOptions

    33

    35	    private const double BoundHeightDefault = 280;

    99	        if (MatchBoundsToSize && _elementSize is null)

   112	    /// <summary>

   128	    protected string[] GetChartLabels()

   131	            ? ChartSeries.Select(ds => ds.Name).ToArray()

   134	
   135	    /// <summary>

   138	    /// <param name="aggregation">The aggregation option.</param>
   139	    /// <returns>An array of aggregated data.</returns>
   140	    protected T[] AggregateSeriesData(AggregationOption aggregation)
   141	    {
   142	        if (aggregation == AggregationOption.None || ChartSeries is null || ChartSeries.Count == 0 || !ChartSeries.Any(x => x.Visible))
   143	        {
   144	            return [];
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        var maxCategoryLength = ChartOptions!.AggregationOption == AggregationOption.GroupByLabel
   148	                ? GetMaxCategoryLengthForLabelGrouping()
   149	                : ChartSeries.Count;
   150	
   151	        var aggregated = new T[maxCategoryLength];
   152	
   153	        return aggregation switch
   154	        {
   155	            AggregationOption.GroupByLabel => AggregateByLabel(aggregated),
   156	            AggregationOption.GroupByDataSet => AggregateByDataSet(aggregated),
   157	            _ => throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(aggregation), $@"Unsupported aggregation: {aggregation}")
   158	        };
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    private int GetMaxCategoryLengthForLabelGrouping()
   162	    {
   163	        return ChartLabels.Length > 0
   164	            ? ChartLabels.Length
   165	            : ChartSeries.Where(x => x.Data?.Values != null).DefaultIfEmpty()
   166	                          .Max(x => x?.Data?.Values.Count ?? 0);
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    private T[] AggregateByLabel(T[] aggregated)
   170	    {
   171	        foreach (var series in ChartSeries.Where(s => s.Visible))
   172	        {
   173	            var values = series.Data?.Values ?? [];
   174	
   175	            for (var i = 0; i < values.Count; i++)
   176	            {
   177	                if (!HiddenIndices.Contains(i) && i < aggregated.Length)
   178	                {
   179	                    aggregated[i] += values[i];
   180	                }
   181	            }
   182	        }
   183	
   184	        return aggregated;
   185	    }
   186	
   187	    private T[] AggregateByDataSet(T[] aggregated)
   188	    {
   189	        var chartSeries = ChartSeries.Take(aggregated.Length);
   190	
   191	        foreach (var (series, index) in chartSeries.Select((s, i) => (s, i)))
   192	        {
   193	            if (!series.Visible)
   194	            {
   195	                continue;
   196	            }
   197	
   198	            aggregated[index] = series.Data?.Values.SumGeneric() ?? T.Zero;
   199	        }
   200	
   201	        return aggregated;
   202	    }
   203	
   204	    /// <summary>
   205	    /// Builds the legends for the chart.
   206	    /// </summary>
   207	    /// <param name="chartLabels">The labels for the chart.</param>
   208	    protected void BuildLegends(string[] chartLabels)
   209	    {
   210	        var isGrouped = ChartOptions!.AggregationOption == AggregationOption.GroupByLabel;
   211	        var indicesWithPaths = _paths.Select(p => p.Index).ToHashSet();
   212	
   213	        for (var i = 0; i < chartLabels.Length; i++)
   214	        {
   215	            var label = chartLabels[i];
   216	
   217	            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(label))
   218	            {
   219	                continue;
   220	            }
   221	
   222	            var hasPath = indicesWithPaths.Contains(i);
   223	
   224	            var visible = isGrouped
   225	                ? !HiddenIndices.Contains(i) && hasPath
   226	                : i < ChartSeries.Count && ChartSeries[i].Visible;
   227	
   228	            if (!CanHideSeries && !visible)
   229	            {
   230	                continue;
   231	            }
   232	
   233	            _legends.Add(new SvgLegend
   234	            {
   235	                Index = i,
   236	                Labels = label,
   237	                Visible = visible,
   238	                OnVisibilityChanged = EventCallback.Factory.Create<SvgLegend>(this, HandleLegendVisibilityChanged)
   239	            });
   240	        }
   241	    }
   242	
   243	    /// <summary>
   244	    /// Sets the bounds of the chart.
   245	    /// </summary>
   246	    protected void SetBounds()
   247	    {
   248	        _boundWidth = BoundWidthDefault;
   249	        _boundHeight = BoundHeightDefault;
   250	
   251	        if (MatchBoundsToSize)
   252	        {
   253	            if (_elementSize is not null)
   254	            {
   255	                _boundWidth = _elementSize.Width;
   256	                _boundHeight = _elementSize.Height;
   257	            }
   258	            else if (Width.EndsWith("px")
   259	                && Height.EndsWith("px")
   260	                && double.TryParse(Width.AsSpan(0, Width.Length - 2), out var width)
   261	                && double.TryParse(Height.AsSpan(0, Height.Length - 2), out var height))
   262	            {
   263	                _boundWidth = width;
   264	                _boundHeight = height;
   265	            }
   266	        }
   267	    }
   268	
   269	    /// <summary>
   270	    /// Scales the input data to the range between 0 and 1
   271	    /// </summary>
   272	    protected double[] GetNormalizedData()
   273	    {
   274	        if (ChartSeries is null || ChartSeries.Count == 0)
   275	        {
   276	            return [];
   277	        }
   278	
   279	        var data = AggregateSeriesData(ChartOptions!.AggregationOption);
   280	        var total = double.CreateSaturating(data.SumGeneric());
   281	
   282	        return total == 0.0 ? (new double[data.Length]) : data.Select(x => double.CreateSaturating(T.Abs(x)) / total).ToArray();
   283	    }
   284	
   285	    /// <summary>
   286	    /// Handles the visibility change of a legend.
   287	    /// </summary>
   288	    /// <param name="legend">The legend whose visibility changed.</param>
   289	    protected void HandleLegendVisibilityChanged(SvgLegend legend)
   290	    {
   291	        if (legend.Visible)
   292	        {
   293	            HiddenIndices.Remove(legend.Index);
   294	        }
   295	        else
   296	        {
   297	            HiddenIndices.Add(legend.Index);
   298	        }
   299	
   300	        if (ChartOptions!.AggregationOption == AggregationOption.GroupByDataSet)
   301	        {
   302	            ChartSeries[legend.Index].Visible = legend.Visible;
   303	        }
   304	
   305	        RebuildChart();
   306	    }
   307	
   308	    /// <summary>
   309	    /// Represents the coordinates of a segment in a radial chart.
   310	    /// </summary>
   311	    protected readonly struct SegmentCoordinates
   312	    {
   313	        /// <summary>
   314	        /// The starting X coordinate.
   315	        /// </summary>
   316	        public double StartX { get; init; }
   317	        /// <summary>
   318	        /// The starting Y coordinate.
   319	        /// </summary>
   320	        public double StartY { get; init; }
   321	        /// <summary>
   322	        /// The middle X coordinate.
   323	        /// </summary>
   324	        public double MidX { get; init; }
   325	        /// <summary>
   326	        /// The middle Y coordinate.
   327	        /// </summary>
   328	        public double MidY { get; init; }
   329	        /// <summary>
   330	        /// The ending X coordinate.
   331	        /// </summary>
   332	        public double EndX { get; init; }
   333	        /// <summary>
   334	        /// The ending Y coordinate.
   335	        /// </summary>
   336	        public double EndY { get; init; }
   337	        /// <summary>
   338	        /// The large arc flag for SVG path.
   339	        /// </summary>
   340	        public int LargeArcFlag { get; init; }
   341	    }
   342	
   343	    /// <summary>
   344	    /// Handles the mouse over event for a segment.
   345	    /// </summary>
   346	    /// <param name="args">The mouse event arguments.</param>
   347	    /// <param name="segment">The hovered segment path.</param>
   348	    internal virtual void OnSegmentMouseOver(MouseEventArgs args, SvgPath segment) => _hoveredSegment = segment;
   349	
   350	    /// <summary>
   351	    /// Handles the mouse out event for a segment.
   352	    /// </summary>
   353	    internal virtual void OnSegmentMouseOut() => _hoveredSegment = null;
   354	
   355	    /// <summary>
   356	    /// Called when the element size changes.
   357	    /// </summary>
   358	    /// <param name="elementSize">The new element size.</param>
   359	    [JSInvokable]
   360	    public void OnElementSizeChanged(ElementSize elementSize)
   361	    {
   362	        if (elementSize == null || elementSize.Timestamp <= _elementSize?.Timestamp)
   363	        {
   364	            return;
   365	        }
   366	
   367	        _elementSize = elementSize;
   368	
   369	        if (!MatchBoundsToSize)
   370	        {
   371	            return;
   372	        }
   373	
   374	        var minDimension = Math.Min(_elementSize.Width, _elementSize.Height);
   375	        _boundWidth = minDimension;
   376	        _boundHeight = minDimension;
   377	
   378	        _debouncer.DebounceAsync(async () =>
   379	        {
   380	            await InvokeAsync(() =>
   381	            {
   382	                RebuildChart();
   383	                StateHasChanged();
   384	            });
   385	        }).CatchAndLog();
   386	    }
   387	
   388	    /// <summary>
   389	    /// Releases the resources used by the component.
   390	    /// </summary>
   391	    public void Dispose()
   392	    {
   393	        Dispose(true);
   394	        GC.SuppressFinalize(this);
   395	    }
   396	
   397	    /// <summary>
   398	    /// Releases the unmanaged resources used by the component and optionally releases the managed resources.
   399	    /// </summary>
   400	    /// <param name="disposing">True to release both managed and unmanaged resources; false to release only unmanaged resources.</param>
   401	    protected virtual void Dispose(bool disposing)
   402	    {
   403	        if (disposing)
   404	        {
   405	            _debouncer.Dispose();
   406	        }
   407	
   408	        _dotNetObjectReference.Dispose();
   409	    }
   410	}

    11	/// <summary>
    12	/// Serves as the base class for axis-based charts, providing core functionality for rendering and managing chart
    13	/// elements such as axes, grids, and legends.
    14	/// </summary>
    15	/// <remarks>
    16	/// Provides foundational features for axis-based charts, including support for shared data
    17	/// regions, overlay charts, and dynamic resizing.
    18	/// </remarks>
    19	/// <typeparam name="T">The type of numeric values used by the chart</typeparam>
    20	/// <typeparam name="TOptions">The type of chart options used to configure the chart's behavior and appearance.</typeparam>
    21	public abstract class MudAxisChartBase<T, TOptions> : MudChartBase<T, TOptions>, IMudAxisChart<T>, IDisposable
    22	    where T : struct, INumber<T>, IMinMaxValue<T>, IFormattable
    23	    where TOptions : IAxisChartOptions

    33	    /// Values are shared between the overlay and the main chart.

   205	    /// <summary>
