   210	        DebouncedRebuild();
   211	    }
   212	
   213	    /// <summary>
   214	    /// Sets the bounds of the chart.
   215	    /// </summary>
   216	    protected void SetBounds()
   217	    {
   218	        if (ChartReference is IMudAxisChart<T> chart && chart.SharedData is { } data)
   219	        {
   220	            _boundWidth = data.BoundWidth;
   221	            _boundHeight = data.BoundHeight;
   222	            return;
   223	        }
   224	
   225	        _boundWidth = BoundWidthDefault;
   226	        _boundHeight = BoundHeightDefault;
   227	
   228	        if (MatchBoundsToSize)
   229	        {
   230	            if (_elementSize is not null)
   231	            {
   232	                _boundWidth = _elementSize.Width;
   233	                _boundHeight = _elementSize.Height;
   234	            }
   235	            else if (Width.AsSpan().Trim().EndsWith("px", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
   236	                && Height.AsSpan().Trim().EndsWith("px", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
   237	                && double.TryParse(Width.AsSpan(0, Width.Length - 2), NumberStyles.Float, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out var width)
   238	                && double.TryParse(Height.AsSpan(0, Height.Length - 2), NumberStyles.Float, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out var height))
   239	            {
   240	                _boundWidth = width;
   241	                _boundHeight = height;
   242	            }
   243	        }
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    /// <summary>
   247	    /// Generates the horizontal grid lines for the chart.
   248	    /// </summary>
   249	    /// <param name="numHorizontalLines">The number of horizontal lines.</param>
   250	    /// <param name="lowestHorizontalLine">The lowest horizontal line.</param>
   251	    /// <param name="gridYUnits">The Y-axis grid units.</param>
   252	    /// <param name="verticalSpace">The vertical space between lines.</param>
   253	    protected void GenerateHorizontalGridLines(int numHorizontalLines, int lowestHorizontalLine, T gridYUnits, double verticalSpace)
   254	    {
   255	        HorizontalLines.Clear();
   256	        HorizontalValues.Clear();
   257	
   258	        for (var i = 0; i < numHorizontalLines; i++)
   259	        {
   260	            var y = VerticalStartSpace + (i * verticalSpace);
   261	            var line = new SvgPath()
   262	            {
   263	                Index = i,
   264	                Data = $"M {ToS(HorizontalStartSpace)} {ToS(_boundHeight - y)} L {ToS(_boundWidth - HorizontalEndSpace)} {ToS(_boundHeight - y)}"
   265	            };
   266	            HorizontalLines.Add(line);
   267	
   268	            var startGridY = T.CreateSaturating(lowestHorizontalLine + i) * gridYUnits;
   269	            var lineValue = new SvgText()
   270	            {
   271	                X = HorizontalStartSpace - 10,
   272	                Y = _boundHeight - y + 5,
   273	                Value = BuildYAxisValueString(startGridY)
   274	            };
   275	            HorizontalValues.Add(lineValue);
   276	        }
   277	    }
   278	
   279	    /// <summary>
   280	    /// Generates the legends for the chart.
   281	    /// </summary>
   282	    protected void GenerateLegends()
   283	    {
   284	        Legends.Clear();
   285	        for (var i = 0; i < Series.Count; i++)
   286	        {
   287	            var series = Series[i];
   288	            var legend = new SvgLegend()
   289	            {
   290	                Index = i,
   291	                Labels = series.Name,
   292	                Visible = series.Visible,
   293	                OnVisibilityChanged = EventCallback.Factory.Create<SvgLegend>(this, HandleLegendVisibilityChanged)
   294	            };
   295	            Legends.Add(legend);
   296	        }
   297	
   298	        if (OverlayChart is IMudAxisChart<T> overlay)
   299	        {
   300	            for (var i = 0; i < overlay.ChartSeries.Count; i++)
   301	            {
   302	                var series = overlay.ChartSeries[i];
   303	                var legend = new SvgLegend()
   304	                {
   305	                    Index = Series.Count + i,
   306	                    Labels = series.Name,
   307	                    Visible = series.Visible,
   308	                    OnVisibilityChanged = EventCallback.Factory.Create<SvgLegend>(this, args => HandleOverlayChartLegendVisibility(overlay, i, args.Visible))
   309	                };
   310	                Legends.Add(legend);
   311	            }
   312	        }
   313	    }
   314	
   315	    /// <summary>
   316	    /// Builds the string for a Y-axis value.
   317	    /// </summary>
   318	    /// <param name="value">The value to build the string for.</param>
   319	    /// <returns>The string representation of the Y-axis value.</returns>
   320	    protected string BuildYAxisValueString(T value)
   321	    {
   322	        var doubleValue = double.CreateSaturating(value);
   323	
   324	        return ChartOptions?.YAxisToStringFunc is null
   325	            ? ToS(doubleValue, ChartOptions?.YAxisFormat)
   326	            : ChartOptions.YAxisToStringFunc(doubleValue);
   327	    }
   328	
   329	    /// <summary>
   330	    /// Formats the tooltip text.
   331	    /// </summary>
   332	    /// <param name="format">The format string.</param>
   333	    /// <param name="series">The chart series.</param>
   334	    /// <param name="path">The SVG path.</param>
   335	    /// <returns>The formatted tooltip text.</returns>
   336	    protected static string FormatTooltipText(string? format, ChartSeries<T> series, SvgPath path)
   337	    {
   338	        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(format))
   339	            return string.Empty;
   340	
   341	        return format
   342	            .Replace("{{SERIES_NAME}}", series.Name)
   343	            .Replace("{{X_VALUE}}", path.LabelXValue)
   344	            .Replace("{{Y_VALUE}}", path.LabelYValue);
   345	    }
   346	
   347	    /// <summary>
   348	    /// Called when the element size changes.
   349	    /// </summary>
   350	    /// <param name="elementSize">The new element size.</param>
   351	    [JSInvokable]
   352	    public void OnElementSizeChanged(ElementSize elementSize)
   353	    {
   354	        if (elementSize is null || elementSize.Timestamp <= _elementSize?.Timestamp)
   355	            return;
   356	
   357	        _elementSize = elementSize;
   358	
   359	        if (!MatchBoundsToSize)
   360	            return;
   361	
   362	        if (Math.Abs(_boundWidth - _elementSize.Width) < Epsilon &&
   363	            Math.Abs(_boundHeight - _elementSize.Height) < Epsilon)
   364	        {
   365	            return;
   366	        }
   367	
   368	        // Debounce the chart update logic
   369	        DebouncedRebuild();
   370	    }
   371	
   372	    private void DebouncedRebuild()
   373	    {
   374	        _debouncer.DebounceAsync(async () =>
   375	        {
   376	            await InvokeAsync(() =>
   377	            {
   378	                RebuildChart();
   379	                StateHasChanged();
   380	            });
   381	        }).CatchAndLog();
   382	    }
   383	
   384	    /// <summary>
   385	    /// Handles the visibility change of a legend.
   386	    /// </summary>
   387	    /// <param name="legend">The legend whose visibility changed.</param>
   388	    protected virtual void HandleLegendVisibilityChanged(SvgLegend legend)
   389	    {
   390	        var series = Series[legend.Index];
   391	        series.Visible = legend.Visible;
   392	        RebuildChart();
   393	    }
   394	
   395	    /// <summary>
   396	    /// Handles the visibility of an overlay chart legend.
   397	    /// </summary>
   398	    /// <param name="overlayChart">The overlay chart.</param>
   399	    /// <param name="index">The index of the series.</param>
   400	    /// <param name="isVisible">Whether the series is visible.</param>
   401	    protected void HandleOverlayChartLegendVisibility(IMudChart<T> overlayChart, int index, bool isVisible)
   402	    {
   403	        if (overlayChart?.ChartSeries != null && index >= 0 && index < overlayChart.ChartSeries.Count)
   404	        {
   405	            overlayChart.ChartSeries[index].Visible = isVisible;
   406	            overlayChart.RebuildChart();
   407	            StateHasChanged();
   408	        }
   409	    }
   410	
   411	    public void Dispose()
   412	    {
   413	        Dispose(true);
   414	        GC.SuppressFinalize(this);
   415	    }
   416	
   417	    protected virtual void Dispose(bool disposing)
   418	    {
   419	        if (disposing)
   420	        {
   421	            _debouncer.Dispose();
   422	        }
   423	
   424	        _dotNetObjectReference.Dispose();
   425	    }
   426	}

   174	        {
   175	            await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);
   176	
   177	            if (firstRender)
   178	            {
   179	                var elementSize = await JsRuntime.InvokeAsync<ElementSize>("mudObserveElementSize", _dotNetObjectReference, _elementReference);
   180	                OnElementSizeChanged(elementSize);
   181	            }
   182	        }
   183	
   184	        private void UpdateLegendPosition(Position position)
   185	        {
   186	            _legendPosition = position switch
   187	            {
   188	                Position.Center => Position.Bottom,
   189	                Position.Start => Position.Left,
   190	                Position.End => Position.Right,
   191	                _ => position
   192	            };
   193	        }
   194	
   195	        private void UpdateChartOptions(HeatMapChartOptions chartOptions)
   196	        {
   197	            if (_options == null || _options != chartOptions)
   198	            {
   199	                _options = chartOptions;
   200	                _colorPalette = _options.ChartPalette.Length > 0 ? _options.ChartPalette : _colorPalette;
   201	            }
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        private void UpdateChartSeries(List<ChartSeries<T>> chartSeriesList)
   205	        {
   206	            var hasUpdatedList = chartSeriesList.Count > 0 && _series != chartSeriesList;
   207	
   208	            if (_series.Count == 0 || hasUpdatedList)
   209	            {
   210	                _series.Clear();
   211	                _series = chartSeriesList;
   212	            }
   213	        }
   214	
   215	        private void UpdateHeatMapCells(List<MudHeatMapCell<T>> mudHeatMapCellsList)
   216	        {
   217	            var hasUpdatedList = mudHeatMapCellsList.Count > 0 && _customHeatMapCells != mudHeatMapCellsList;
   218	
   219	            if (_customHeatMapCells.Count == 0 || hasUpdatedList)
   220	            {
   221	                _customHeatMapCells.Clear();
   222	                _customHeatMapCells = mudHeatMapCellsList;
   223	            }
   224	
   225	            var padding = _options is { EnableSmoothGradient: true } ? 0 : CellPadding;
   226	
   227	            if (RowCount == 0 || SeriesLength == 0)
   228	            {
   229	                _cellDimension = new CellDimension(CellMinSize, CellMinSize, padding);
   230	                return;
   231	            }
   232	
   233	            var cellHeight = Math.Max(CellMinSize, (_boundHeight - _verticalStartSpace - _verticalEndSpace - (padding * (RowCount - 1))) / RowCount);
   234	            var cellWidth = Math.Max(CellMinSize, (_boundWidth - _horizontalStartSpace - _horizontalEndSpace - (padding * (SeriesLength - 1))) / SeriesLength);
   235	
   236	            _cellDimension = new CellDimension(cellWidth, cellHeight, padding);
   237	        }
   238	
   239	        public override void RebuildChart()
   240	        {
   241	            SetBounds();
   242	            // Populate _heatmapCells based on data, e.g., matrix of values
   243	            _heatMapCells.Clear();
   244	            _toggleLegend.Clear();
   245	            _minValue = T.MaxValue;
   246	            _maxValue = T.MinValue;
   247	
   248	            var hasValues = false;
   249	            // # of rows
   250	            var rows = _series.Count;
   251	            // cols should be the max number of data[] in all series
   252	            var cols = SeriesLength;
   253	
   254	            for (var row = 0; row < rows; row++)
   255	            {
   256	                for (var col = 0; col < cols; col++)
   257	                {
   258	                    var mudHeatMapOverride = _customHeatMapCells.FirstOrDefault(x => x.Row == row && x.Column == col);
   259	                    var value = mudHeatMapOverride?.Value ?? GetDataValue(row, col); // Method to retrieve the value for each cell                    
   260	                    _heatMapCells.Add(new HeatMapCell<T>
   261	                    {
   262	                        Row = row,
   263	                        Column = col,
   264	                        Value = value,
   265	                        CustomFragment = mudHeatMapOverride?.ChildContent,
   266	                        Width = mudHeatMapOverride?.Width,
   267	                        Height = mudHeatMapOverride?.Height,
   268	                        MudColor = mudHeatMapOverride?.MudColor,
   269	                    });
   270	                    if (value.HasValue)
   271	                    {
   272	                        _minValue = T.Min(_minValue, value.Value);
   273	                        _maxValue = T.Max(_maxValue, value.Value);
   274	                        hasValues = true;
   275	                    }
   276	                }
   277	
   278	                if (CanHideSeries)
   279	                {
   280	                    var legend = new SvgLegend
   281	                    {
   282	                        Index = row,
   283	                        Labels = _series[row].Name,
   284	                        Visible = _series[row].Visible,
   285	                        OnVisibilityChanged = EventCallback.Factory.Create<SvgLegend>(this, HandleLegendVisibilityChanged)
   286	                    };
   287	                    _toggleLegend.Add(legend);
   288	                }
   289	            }
   290	
   291	            var overrideMinValue = _customHeatMapCells.LastOrDefault(x => x.MinValue.HasValue)?.MinValue;
   292	            var overrideMaxValue = _customHeatMapCells.LastOrDefault(x => x.MaxValue.HasValue)?.MaxValue;
   293	
   294	            _minValue = overrideMinValue ?? (hasValues ? _minValue : T.Zero);
   295	            _maxValue = overrideMaxValue ?? (hasValues ? _maxValue : T.One);
   296	
   297	            CalculateAreas();
   298	            BuildLegends();
   299	            UpdateHeatMapCells(MudHeatMapCells);
   300	            StateHasChanged();
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        private void HandleLegendVisibilityChanged(SvgLegend legend)
   304	        {
   305	            var series = _series[legend.Index];
   306	            series.Visible = legend.Visible;
   307	            RebuildChart();
   308	        }
   309	
   310	        private void CalculateAreas()
   311	        {
   312	            // Defaults each side gets some space around the heatmap
   313	            _verticalStartSpace = _verticalEndSpace = _horizontalStartSpace = _horizontalEndSpace = HeatMapPadding;
   314	            var estimatedCellWidth = Math.Max(CellMinSize, (_boundWidth - (6 * HeatMapPadding) - CellPadding) / Math.Max(1, SeriesLength));
   315	            var estimatedCellHeight = (_boundHeight - (6 * HeatMapPadding)) / Math.Max(1, RowCount);
   316	            _dynamicFontSize = CalculateFontSize(estimatedCellWidth, estimatedCellHeight, 8);
   317	
   318	            // Calculate Y-axis label width based on dynamic font size
   319	            _yAxisLabelWidth = (_series.Count > 0 ? _series.Max(x => x.Name.Length) : 1) * _dynamicFontSize * AverageCharWidthMultiplier;
   320	
   321	            const double DefaultCharsWidth = 5 * LegendFontSize * AverageCharWidthMultiplier;
   322	            _legendLabelsYAxis = (int)Math.Ceiling(_options is { ShowLegendLabels: true }
   323	                ? DefaultCharsWidth + LegendLineLength
   324	                : 0);
   325	            _legendLabelsXAxis = _options is { ShowLegendLabels: true }
   326	                ? LegendFontSize + LegendLineLength
   327	                : 0;
   328	
   329	            // make room for X and Y Axis Labels
   330	            if (_options?.YAxisLabelPosition == YAxisLabelPosition.Left)
   331	            {
   332	                _horizontalStartSpace += CellPadding + _yAxisLabelWidth + CellPadding;
   333	            }
   334	
   335	            if (_options?.YAxisLabelPosition == YAxisLabelPosition.Right)
   336	            {
   337	                _horizontalEndSpace += CellPadding + _yAxisLabelWidth + CellPadding;
   338	            }
   339	
   340	            if (_options?.XAxisLabelPosition == XAxisLabelPosition.Top)
   341	            {
   342	                _verticalStartSpace += CellPadding + _dynamicFontSize + CellPadding;
   343	            }
   344	
   345	            if (_options?.XAxisLabelPosition == XAxisLabelPosition.Bottom)
   346	            {
   347	                _verticalEndSpace += CellPadding + _dynamicFontSize + CellPadding;
   348	            }
   349	
   350	            // Make Room for Legend (if Any)
   351	            if (_options is { ShowLegend: true })
   352	            {
   353	                switch (_legendPosition)
   354	                {
   355	                    case Position.Bottom:
   356	                        _verticalEndSpace += CellPadding + _legendLabelsXAxis + LegendBox + CellPadding;
   357	                        break;
   358	
   359	                    case Position.Top:
   360	                        _verticalStartSpace += CellPadding + _legendLabelsXAxis + LegendBox + CellPadding;
   361	                        break;
   362	
   363	                    case Position.Left:
   364	                        _horizontalStartSpace += CellPadding + _legendLabelsYAxis + LegendBox + CellPadding;
   365	                        break;
   366	
   367	                    case Position.Right:
   368	                        _horizontalEndSpace += CellPadding + _legendLabelsYAxis + LegendBox + CellPadding;
   369	                        break;
   370	                }
   371	            }
   372	        }
   373	
   374	        private void BuildLegends()
   375	        {
   376	            _legends.Clear();
   377	            var colors = GetEqualizedColorPalette(5); // Always generate 5 shades
   378	
   379	            for (var i = 0; i < colors.Length; i++)
   380	            {
   381	                var t = i / (double)(colors.Length - 1);
   382	                var value = _minValue + (T.CreateSaturating(t) * (_maxValue - _minValue));
   383	                _legends.Add((value, colors[i].ToString(MudColorOutputFormats.RGB)));
   384	            }
   385	        }
   386	
   387	        private T? GetDataValue(int row, int col)
   388	        {
   389	            // need to ensure row index exists in case there is no data for a row in a series
   390	            if (row < 0 || row >= _series.Count)
   391	            {
   392	                return null;
   393	            }
   394	
   395	            // need to ensure column index exists in case there is no data for a column in a series
   396	            if (col < 0 || _series[row].Data == null || col >= _series[row].Data.Values.Count)
   397	            {
   398	                return null;
   399	            }
   400	
   401	            return _series[row].Data[col].Y;
   402	        }
   403	
   404	        private string GetColorForValue(T? value)
   405	        {
   406	            if (value is null)
   407	            {
   408	                return "#fff"; // Default color for missing data
   409	            }
   410	
   411	            var range = _maxValue - _minValue;
   412	            var offset = value.Value - _minValue;
   413	
   414	            // Find the closest matching color in the legends
   415	            var normalizedValue = Math.Clamp(double.CreateSaturating(offset / range), 0.0, 1.0);
   416	            var legendIndex = (int)Math.Floor(normalizedValue * (_legends.Count - 1));
   417	            return _legends[Math.Clamp(legendIndex, 0, _legends.Count - 1)].color;
   418	        }
   419	
   420	        private MudColor[] GetEqualizedColorPalette(int shadeCount)
   421	        {
   422	            var baseColors = _colorPalette.Select(x => new MudColor(x)).ToArray();
   423	            var colorCount = baseColors.Length;
   424	
   425	            if (colorCount == 1)
   426	            {
   427	                return MudColor.GenerateTintShadePalette(baseColors[0]).ToArray();
   428	            }
   429	
   430	            if (colorCount != 5)
   431	            {
   432	                return MudColor.GenerateMultiGradientPalette(baseColors, shadeCount).ToArray();
   433	            }
   434	
   435	            return baseColors;
   436	        }
   437	
   438	        private string FormatValueForDisplay(T? value)
   439	        {
   440	            if (value == null)
   441	                return string.Empty;
   442	
   443	            var formatString = _options?.ValueFormatString ?? "G";
   444	            // Format the value and truncate to 5 characters or fewer
   445	            var formattedValue = value.Value.ToString(formatString, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
   446	
   447	            return formattedValue.Length > 5 ? formattedValue[..5] : formattedValue;
   448	        }
   449	
   450	        private static double CalculateFontSize(double cellWidth, double cellHeight, int defaultSize)
   451	        {
   452	            var minDimension = Math.Min(cellWidth, cellHeight);
   453	
   454	            return Math.Max(defaultSize, 2 * Math.Sqrt(minDimension));
   455	        }
   456	
   457	        private (double x, double y) GetLegendPosition()
   458	        {
   459	            // Determine the horizontal position based on the legend's position.
   460	            var x = _legendPosition switch
   461	            {
   462	                Position.Top or Position.Bottom => _horizontalStartSpace + (HeatmapWidth / 2),
   463	                Position.Right => GetRightPosition(),
   464	                Position.Left => GetLeftPosition(),
   465	                _ => 0
   466	            };
   467	
   468	            // Determine the vertical position based on the legend's position.
   469	            var y = _legendPosition switch
   470	            {
   471	                Position.Right or Position.Left => _verticalStartSpace + (HeatmapHeight / 2),
   472	                Position.Bottom => GetBottomPosition(),
   473	                Position.Top => GetTopPosition(),
   474	                _ => 0
   475	            };
   476	
   477	            return (x, y);
   478	
   479	            // Calculates the horizontal position for the legend when it is placed on the right.
   480	            double GetRightPosition() =>
   481	                _horizontalStartSpace + HeatmapWidth + HeatMapPadding +
   482	                (_options?.YAxisLabelPosition == YAxisLabelPosition.Right ? _yAxisLabelWidth + CellPadding : 0);
   483	
   484	            // Calculates the horizontal position for the legend when it is placed on the left.
   485	            double GetLeftPosition() =>
   486	                _horizontalStartSpace - HeatMapPadding - LegendBox -
   487	                (_options?.YAxisLabelPosition == YAxisLabelPosition.Left ? _yAxisLabelWidth + CellPadding : 0);
   488	
   489	            // Calculates the vertical position for the legend when it is placed at the bottom.
   490	            double GetBottomPosition() =>
   491	                _verticalStartSpace + HeatmapHeight + HeatMapPadding + CellPadding + CellPadding +
   492	                (_options?.XAxisLabelPosition == XAxisLabelPosition.Bottom ? _dynamicFontSize : 0);
   493	
   494	            // Calculates the vertical position for the legend when it is placed at the top.
   495	            double GetTopPosition() =>
   496	                _verticalStartSpace - CellPadding - LegendBox -
   497	                (_options?.XAxisLabelPosition == XAxisLabelPosition.Top ? _dynamicFontSize + CellPadding : 0);
   498	        }
   499	
   500	        internal List<MudHeatMapCell<T>> MudHeatMapCells { get; set; } = [];
   501	
   502	        internal void AddCell(MudHeatMapCell<T> cell)
   503	        {
   504	            MudHeatMapCells.Add(cell);
   505	
   506	            DebouncedRebuild();
   507	        }
   508	
   509	        private void SetBounds()
   510	        {
   511	            _boundWidth = BoundWidth;
   512	            _boundHeight = BoundHeight;
   513	
   514	            if (MatchBoundsToSize)
   515	            {
   516	                if (_elementSize is not null)
   517	                {
   518	                    _boundWidth = _elementSize.Width;
   519	                    _boundHeight = _elementSize.Height;
   520	                }
   521	                else if (Width.EndsWith("px")
   522	                         && Height.EndsWith("px")
   523	                         && double.TryParse(Width.AsSpan(0, Width.Length - 2), out var width)
   524	                         && double.TryParse(Height.AsSpan(0, Height.Length - 2), out var height))
   525	                {
   526	                    _boundWidth = width;
   527	                    _boundHeight = height;
   528	                }
   529	            }
   530	        }
   531	
   532	        [JSInvokable]
   533	        public void OnElementSizeChanged(ElementSize elementSize)
   534	        {
   535	            if (elementSize == null || elementSize.Timestamp <= _elementSize?.Timestamp)
   536	                return;
   537	
   538	            _elementSize = elementSize;
   539	
   540	            if (!MatchBoundsToSize)
   541	                return;
   542	
   543	            if (Math.Abs(_boundWidth - _elementSize.Width) < Epsilon &&
   544	                Math.Abs(_boundHeight - _elementSize.Height) < Epsilon)
   545	            {
   546	                return;
   547	            }
   548	
   549	            DebouncedRebuild();
   550	        }
   551	
   552	        private void DebouncedRebuild()
   553	        {
   554	            _debouncer.DebounceAsync(async () =>
   555	            {
   556	                await InvokeAsync(RebuildChart);
   557	            }).CatchAndLog();
   558	        }
   559	
   560	        private void OnCellMouseOver(HeatMapCell<T>? cell)
   561	        {
   562	            _hoveredCell = cell;
   563	        }
   564	
   565	        private void OnCellMouseOut()
   566	        {
   567	            _hoveredCell = null;
   568	        }
   569	
   570	        private void OnLegendMouseOver((T value, string color) legend, PointF position)
   571	        {
   572	            _hoveredLegend = legend;
   573	            _hoveredLegendPosition = position;
   574	        }
   575	
   576	        private void OnLegendMouseOut()
   577	        {
   578	            _hoveredLegend = null;
   579	        }
   580	
   581	        internal async Task SetSelectedCellAsync(int row, int column)
   582	        {
   583	            SelectedCell = (row, column);
   584	
   585	            await SetSelectedIndexAsync(row);
   586	        }
   587	
   588	        public void Dispose()
   589	        {
   590	            Dispose(true);
   591	            GC.SuppressFinalize(this);
   592	        }
   593	
   594	        protected virtual void Dispose(bool disposing)
   595	        {
   596	            if (!disposing) return;
   597	
   598	            _debouncer.Dispose();
   599	            _dotNetObjectReference?.Dispose();
   600	        }
   601	    }
   602	}

Now I have a clear picture. Let me look at the PR description again:

The PR says: "MudTextField provides access to both DebounceInterval and OnDebounceIntervalElapsed, whereas MudAutocomplete only exposes DebounceInterval."

From my analysis:
- `MudTextField` inherits from `MudDebouncedInput<T>` which has both `DebounceInterval` (double) and `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` (EventCallback<string>)
- `MudAutocomplete` inherits from `MudBaseInput<T>` directly, has its own `DebounceInterval` (int), and does NOT have `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed`

The fix is to add `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` to `MudAutocomplete`. Let me also check if there are other components that need this change. Let me search for all components that have `DebounceInterval` as a parameter but not `OnDebounceIntervalEl

Now I understand the full picture. The PR description says:

> There is an inconsistency in the usage of OnDebounceIntervalElapsed across components. Specifically, if a component supports the DebounceInterval property, it should also support the OnDebounceIntervalElapsed event. For example, MudTextField provides access to both DebounceInterval and OnDebounceIntervalElapsed, whereas MudAutocomplete only exposes DebounceInterval.

So the fix is to add `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` to `MudAutocomplete`. Let me look at how `MudAutocomplete` uses its debounce timer and where the event should be fired.

Currently in `MudAutocomplete`, the `DebounceInterval` is used in `UpdateValuePropertyAsync`:

```csharp
if (DebounceInterval <= 0)
    await OpenMenuAsync();
else
    _debounceTimer = TimeProvider.CreateTimer(OnDebounceComplete, null, TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(DebounceInterval), Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan);
```

And `OnDebounceComplete` just calls `OpenMenuAsync`.

The `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` should be called when the debounce interval has elapsed, similar to how `MudDebouncedInput` does it.

Let me now implement the changes. First, let me look at the `.razor` file for `MudAutocomplete` to see if there's anything there that needs updating

Now I understand the architecture. `MudAutocomplete` inherits from `MudBaseInput<T>` directly, not from `MudDebouncedInput<T>`. It has its own `DebounceInterval` (int, default 100) and its own debounce timer.

I need to add `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` to `MudAutocomplete`. Let me add the parameter and fire it when the debounce interval elapses.

Let me look at how the debounce works in `MudAutocomplete`:

1. `UpdateValuePropertyAsync` - if `DebounceInterval > 0`, it creates a timer that calls `OnDebounceComplete`
2. `OnDebounceComplete` - calls `InvokeAsync(OpenMenuAsync)`

So the `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` event should be fired before/alongside `OpenMenuAsync` in the `OnDebounceComplete` method.

Now let me think about edge cases:

1. The `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` is only fired when `DebounceInterval > 0` and the timer fires. That's correct - it mirrors the behavior of `MudDebouncedInput`.

2. In `MudDebouncedInput`, the event is fired inside `OnDebouncedUpdate` which is called after the debounce. The event passes `ReadText` as the argument. I'm doing the same in my implementation.

3. What if `DebounceInterval` is 0 or negative? In that case, `OpenMenuAsync()` is called directly without going through `OnDebounceComplete`, so `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` is NOT fired. This is consistent with `MudDebouncedInput` where the debounce only fires when `DebounceInterval > 0`.

Let me verify this behavior in `MudDebouncedInput`:

```csharp
// MudDebouncedInput.UpdateValuePropertyAsync:
if (DebounceInterval <= 0 || _debouncer is null)
{
    return base.UpdateValuePropertyAsync(updateText);
}
// Debounce the update
_ = _debouncer.DebounceAsync(OnDebouncedUpdate);
```

Yes, `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` is only fired when the debounce interval is > 0. This is correct.

Let me also double-check the `OnDebounceComplete` change to ensure it's async-safe. The original code was:

```csharp
private void OnDebounceComplete(object? stateInfo) => InvokeAsync(OpenMenuAsync);
```

My new code is:

```csharp
private void OnDebounceComplete(object? stateInfo) => InvokeAsync(async () =>
{
    await OnDebounceIntervalElapsed.InvokeAsync(ReadText);
    await OpenMenuAsync();
});
```

This should be fine. `InvokeAsync` ensures the code runs on the UI thread. The `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` is invoked first, then `OpenMenuAsync`. This is consistent with `MudDebouncedInput` where `OnDebounceIntervalElapsed` is invoked before `base.UpdateValuePropertyAsync`.
